\par }\pard \qj \li0\ri0\nowidctlpar\faauto\rin0\lin0\itap0 {\f2\fs20\insrsid13266562 EXT./INT. BLACKNESS
\par 
\par We see black, hear nothing. Bubbles fill our view, as we realize that we are zooming out, revealing what appear to be long, tangled white strands. Zooming out even farther, it appears that the tangled strands are DNA inside a cell, and, zooming farther st
ill, the cell is inside a microscopic organism that swarms with several hundred others.
\par 
\par Finally, we zoom out even farther, to reveal that we are looking at a single drop of water dangling on a leaf bud. The drop of water, through the magic of special effects, is isolated, and turns into a spinning model of the planet Earth.
\par 
\par A deep, dark voice overcomes our ears.
\par 
\par }\pard \ql \li3220\ri0\nowidctlpar\faauto\rin0\lin3220\itap0 {\f2\fs20\insrsid13266562 VOICE
\par }\pard \ql \li1420\ri1420\nowidctlpar\faauto\rin1420\lin1420\itap0 {\f2\fs20\insrsid13266562 No one would have believed that in the first years of the 21st century, that our world was being watched by intelligences greater than our own.
\par }\pard \ql \li0\ri0\nowidctlpar\faauto\rin0\lin0\itap0 {\f2\fs20\insrsid13266562 
\par The Earth suddenly turns into a red orb, which than transitions itself into...
\par 
\par EXT. BUSY STREET--DAY
\par 
\par A red streetlight on a busy industrial street. People scurry about their lives, searching for their next destination. The voice occurs again.
\par 
\par }\pard \ql \li3220\ri0\nowidctlpar\faauto\rin0\lin3220\itap0 {\f2\fs20\insrsid13266562 VOICE

That as men busied themselves among their various concerns, they were scrutinized and studied, perhaps the way a man with a microscope might observe the transient creatures that swarm and multiply in a drop of water.
\par }\pard \ql \li0\ri0\nowidctlpar\tx916\tx1832\tx2748\tx3664\tx4580\tx5496\tx6412\tx7328\tx8244\tx9160\tx10076\tx10992\tx11908\tx12824\tx13740\tx14656\faauto\rin0\lin0\itap0 {\f2\fs20\insrsid13266562 
\par EXT. FLASH FOOTAGE OF MONUMENTS--DAY
\par 
\par We see the Arc de Triomphe, Mt. Rushmore, and several other well-known monuments pass by the screen.
\par 
\par }\pard \ql \li3220\ri0\nowidctlpar\tx916\tx1832\tx2748\tx3664\tx4580\tx5496\tx6412\tx7328\tx8244\tx9160\tx10076\tx10992\tx11908\tx12824\tx13740\tx14656\faauto\rin0\lin3220\itap0 {\f2\fs20\insrsid13266562 VOICE

\par EXT. SPACE
\par 
\par The voice carries over from the previous transition. We see the Earth, rotating on its axis majestically.
\par 
\par }\pard \ql \li3220\ri0\nowidctlpar\tx916\tx1832\tx2748\tx3664\tx4580\tx5496\tx6412\tx7328\tx8244\tx9160\tx10076\tx10992\tx11908\tx12824\tx13740\tx14656\faauto\rin0\lin3220\itap0 {\f2\fs20\insrsid13266562 VOICE

\par }\pard \ql \li0\ri0\nowidctlpar\tx916\tx1832\tx2748\tx3664\tx4580\tx5496\tx6412\tx7328\tx8244\tx9160\tx10076\tx10992\tx11908\tx12824\tx13740\tx14656\faauto\rin0\lin0\itap0 {\f2\fs20\insrsid13266562

\par Large bold letters appear, covering the Earth:
\par 
\par \'93WAR OF THE WORLDS.\'94
\par 
\par FADE TO:
\par 
\par EXT. INDUSTRIAL DOCKS--NEW JERSEY SHORE--DAY
\par 
\par We are zooming in on a crane, hanging high above a large cargo ship. The crane is carefully maneuvering large steel crates around the deck of the ship. Other workers dart about, others direct the driver of the crane, who sits in a glass compartment high a
bove.
\par 
\par INT. CRANE CAB--CONTINUE
\par 
\par RAY FERRIER (30\rquote s/40\rquote s) sits comfortably in the seat, working the controls of the crane with two joysticks. He is dressed like a normal dock worker: greasy, dirty, a pullover and beat up New York Yankees baseball cap.
\par 
\par Looking downward through the glass floor, he watches his work carefully.
\par 
\par EXT. INDUSTRIAL DOCKS--LATER--DAY
\par 
\par RAY, with a smile on his face, is walking away from the docks, he throws his hard hat to a passing fellow worker. Behind him, we see his FAT BOSS power-walking towards him.
\par

\par SMASH CUT TO:
\par 
\par EXT. STREET--NEW JERSEY--DAY
\par 
\par Ray\rquote s vintage Ford Mustang comes roaring sharply around a corner, much to the dismay of the law-abiding drivers. They honk at him, but he only speeds up, a bridge to Manhattan looms in the distance.
\par 
\par The Mustang careens around another corner and quickly pulls into a driveway. Stopping on a dime on the pavement. The driveway is at Ray\rquote 
s house, which is lined up with several other identical houses along the street, almost like townhouses, with a tiny alley separating each one. 
\par 
\par There is a brand new SUV parked by Ray\rquote s driveway, standing next to it are a statuesque good-looking man, Tim, and a pregnant woman, Ray\rquote s ex-wife, Mary-Anne.
\par 
\par Ray gets out of his car, awkwardly at the clean cut Tim and his new wife, which was once his.

\par INT. UPSTAIRS HALLWAY--RAY\rquote S HOUSE--DAY
\par 
\par Ray rushes over to an open door, leading to his room. Inside we can see that it is a mess, with the bed unmade and clothes thrown everywhere. He shuts the door and nods towards another open door, leading to Rachel and Robbie\rquote s room.

\par Everything goes silent as we see something appear at the top of the caved-in portion of the ceiling in the corner. Rachel ducks out of the way, Ray stands and watches as a mechanical, snake-like probe slithers down into the basement. It looks like a long,
 metal anaconda.
\par 
\par The end of the probe suddenly opens to reveal a camera-lens eye, and floodlights flash on the sides.
\par 
\par Ray immediately ducks to the side of the couch. He crouches low, sweating as the snake-probe creeps forward into the room, starting a game of cat and mouse.
\par 
\par Rachel is standing behind a tattered curtain, watching cautiously, her breaths short.
\par 
\par Suddenly, a small rat runs across the room, getting the attention of the probe, it follows the rat deep into the basement, allowing Ray time to grab Rachel and stand behind a wall partitioning the basement into two sides.
\par 
\par We see an axe on the wall, and then a hand pick it up. It is Ogilvy, moving slowly towards the body of the probe as it busies itself deep in the basement confines. Ray watches from the other side of the probe, his eyes widen.
\par 
\par Ogilvy raises the axe, preparing to slash the probe\rquote s body, but then glances at Ray. Ray is shaking his head and mouthing \'93no.\'94 Ogilvy lo
wers the axe, thinking, then raises it again. Ray waves Ogilvy over silently, and he finally, and nervously, agrees.
\par 
\par Ogilvy puts the axe to his side and slowly ducks underneath the probe\rquote s body, joining Ray on the other side. But then...he drops the axe. It clanks on the ground, drawing the attention of the probe.
\par 
\par The group run for a corner, and find a large mirror. They set it up quickly and huddle behind it, just in time to remain hidden from the probe. Curiously, the probe looks at its own reflection, closely, examining itself, then slowly starts to move away.

\par 
\par Reverse angle, from behind mirror: as we see the probe moving away, Rachel slips her foot out in the open.
\par 
\par The probe hears this, and whips around, looking for the source of the disturbance. It focuses in on the tip of Rachel\rquote 
s shoe sticking out from behind the mirror. It moves closer, closer, until it reaches the back of the mirror, to reveal a shoe, but not person in it. Looking befuddled, the probe examines the area, and behind it, we see the g
roup move across the room to another hiding spot. 
\par 
\par Finally, the probe, outsmarted, begins to retract back up through the ceiling. As it does, its mechanical eyelid closes and its floodlights go off. We hear nothing but silence and the sound of dripping water.
\par 
\par Ray, Rachel, and Ogilvy sigh in relief for a few brief seconds. Rachel sits down in the chair, panting quietly. Suddenly, our peace is shattered by the sound of moving water.
\par 
\par Looking down one of the slightly flooded passageways, we see the water start to move in waves, as it becomes obvious that someone, or something, is walking through it.
\par 
\par Ray immediately dives in front of the couch as three dark silhouettes move behind it, behind a string of tattered curtains. They appear to look like giant heads mounted on three stilts, producing grunting noises and small bellows.
\par 
\par Abruptly, one of the giant heads pops through the curtains to have a look around, and reveals itself as none ot
her than an alien, with bluish, reptilian skin and two large black eyes. There mouths open sideways, and mounted on the head on stilts are two stubby, nearly useless, arms.
\par 
\par The alien pulls back the chair Rachel is sitting in, but miraculously doesn\rquote t spot
 her frozen body; instead it looks over to two of its buddies, who are going through a box of memorabilia, and heads for them. Ray and Rachel seize the opportunity and head for a corner off screen.
\par 
\par By the aliens, they go through a box of random, dusty things. One of them spins the wheel on a nearby bike hanging on the wall, it jumps back as it falls, accidentally hitting another alien, annoying it.
\par 
\par Focus on across the room, the barrel of Ogilvy\rquote s shotgun comes poking around a corner, aiming for the group of aliens. Suddenly, it jerks back, and the slips back into the corner.
\par 
\par AROUND THE CORNER, Ray struggles against Ogilvy, trying to hold him  from shooting the aliens, a risk getting caught. Ogilvy swings around, holding the shotgun, and pins Ray, who also
 holds the gun, against the wall. Rachel watches on in horror, her glances switching between the struggling men and the aliens.
\par 
\par BY THE ALIENS, they find a picture in the box, upon closer inspection, we see that it is a picture of Ogilvy and his family. They sniff it, examine it, and pass it down amongst each other.
\par 
\par AROUND THE CORNER, Ogilvy stares into Ray\rquote s eyes, as it becomes obvious he is overcoming him. The shotgun barrel starts moving towards the aliens, preparing to fire.
\par 
\par We are overcome by the fam

\par EXT. WIDE SHOT OF BOSTON--DAY
\par 
\par We see many of the tripods, all fallen and smoking, all dead, succumbed to the same mysterious force. We suddenly focus on a nearby tree, and zoom in on in: there is a single green leaf hanging from it.
